[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA heap-buffer-overflow vulnerability has been detected in the libexif library [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mduring fuzzing with AddressSanitizer. The issue occurs when processing EXIF data [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfrom Apple maker notes, specifically in the `exif_get_sshort` function called from [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`exif_mnote_data_apple_load`. The overflow involves a [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte read operation [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mattempting to access memory [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m bytes beyond a [0m[1;36m512[0m[39m-byte allocated heap region.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Vulnerability Type[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis is a **heap-buffer-overflow** vulnerability, specifically a [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte read [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moperation beyond allocated memory boundaries. AddressSanitizer has assigned it a [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mscariness score of [0m[1;36m12[0m[39m, classifying it as a [0m[32m"1-byte-read-heap-buffer-overflow"[0m[39m.[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Issue Details[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability manifests during the following execution flow:[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. The fuzzer invokes `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` with test data[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. This calls `exif_data_new_from_data` to parse EXIF data[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Subsequently, `exif_data_load_data` is called to load the data[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. The flow continues to `exif_mnote_data_apple_load` which processes [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mApple-specific maker note data[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Finally, `exif_get_short` is called, which internally uses `exif_get_sshort`[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. At this point, the overflow occurs at address `[0m[1;36m0x515000000785[0m[39m`[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Memory Access Pattern[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- A [0m[1;36m512[0m[39m-byte region was allocated starting at address `[0m[1;36m0x515000000580[0m[39m` and ending [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mat `[0m[1;36m0x515000000780[0m[39m`[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The problematic read attempts to access address `[0m[1;36m0x515000000785[0m[39m`, which is [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbytes beyond the allocated region[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The shadow byte analysis confirms this is in the heap left redzone [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmarked as [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m'fa'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, indicating freed or inaccessible heap memory[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Stack Trace Analysis[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe critical call chain is:[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexif_get_sshort [0m[1;39m([0m[35m/src/libexif/libexif/[0m[95mexif-utils.c[0m[1;39m)[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m└─ exif_get_short [0m[1;39m([0m[35m/src/libexif/libexif/[0m[95mexif-utils.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;92m104:10[0m[1;39m)[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   └─ exif_mnote_data_apple_load [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[35m/src/libexif/libexif/apple/[0m[95mexif-mnote-data-apple.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;92m110:29[0m[1;39m)[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      └─ exif_data_load_data [0m[1;39m([0m[35m/src/libexif/libexif/[0m[95mexif-data.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;92m1010:2[0m[1;39m)[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         └─ exif_data_new_from_data [0m[1;39m([0m[35m/src/libexif/libexif/[0m[95mexif-data.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;92m159:2[0m[1;39m)[0m        [2m                [0m
